Introduction

The API documentation for Bookshelves to use endpoints with another app.

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://127.0.0.1:8000

Authenticating requests

This API is authenticated by sending an Authorization header with the value "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}".

All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

Account

GET Current user.

requires authentication

Route name: api.v1.profile

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/profile" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/profile"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/profile',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (401):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
vary: Origin
 

{
    "message": "Unauthenticated."
}

Request      

POST api/v1/profile/update

Body Parameters

name  string  

Must not be greater than 256 characters.

email  string  

Must be a valid email address. Must not be greater than 256 characters.

about  string optional  

Must not be greater than 2048 characters.

avatar  string optional  

Must not be greater than 2048 characters.

banner  string optional  

Must not be greater than 2048 characters.

use_gravatar  boolean  

display_favorites  boolean  

display_comments  boolean  

display_gender  boolean  

gender  string optional  

POST Delete current user.

requires authentication

Route name: api.v1.profile.delete

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/profile/delete" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"current_password\": \"enqnhkqwbsacidpjylhp\",
    \"confirm\": false
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/profile/delete"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "current_password": "enqnhkqwbsacidpjylhp",
    "confirm": false
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/profile/delete',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'current_password' => 'enqnhkqwbsacidpjylhp',
            'confirm' => false,
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (401):

content-type: application/json

Request      

POST api/v1/password/update

Body Parameters

current_password  string  

Must not be greater than 256 characters.

password  string  

Must not be greater than 256 characters.

POST Login.

Route name: api.login

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"rhiannon52@example.org\",
    \"password\": \"cumque\",
    \"remember\": true
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/login"
);

Request      

GET api/v1/authors/{author_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.slug authors' list, example: explorer-asp

GET Books list of an author.

Books list from an author, find by slug.

Route name: api.v1.authors.show.books

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/authors/books/audouin-mamikonian-sophie?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/authors/books/audouin-mamikonian-sophie"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/authors/books/audouin-mamikonian-sophie',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

curl --request GET \

    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books"
);

const params = {
    "filter[languages]": "en,fr",
    "sort": "slug_sort",
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books',
    [

            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',

);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/books

Query Parameters

filter[languages]  string optional  

Filter by language, meta.slug from languages' list, null by default.

sort  string optional  

Sorting slug_sort by default, available: title, slug_sort, date, created_at, you can use - before parameter to reverse like -slug_sort.

perPage  int optional  

Number of entities to return in a page.

page  int optional  

Page number to return, 1 by default

Response

Response Fields

List of books.

Links to get other pages.

Metadata about pagination.

GET Book details.

Route name: api.v1.books.show

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books/arnaud-georges-jean/mausolee-pour-une-locomotive-fr" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books/arnaud-georges-jean/mausolee-pour-une-locomotive-fr"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books/arnaud-georges-jean/mausolee-pour-une-locomotive-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/books/{author_slug}/{book_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author books' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to books' list and not authors' list, example: arnaud-georges-jean

book_slug  string  

slug of book in meta.slug books' list, example: mausolee-pour-une-locomotive-fr

GET Book collection related entries.

WITH PAGINATION

Get all Series/Books related to selected Book from Tag/Genre.

Route name: api.v1.books.related

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books/related/bordage-pierre/frere-elthor-fr?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books/related/bordage-pierre/frere-elthor-fr"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books/related/bordage-pierre/frere-elthor-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request failed with error:

Request      

GET api/v1/books/related/{author_slug}/{book_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author books' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to books' list and not authors' list, example: bordage-pierre

book_slug  string  

slug of book in meta.slug books' list, example: frere-elthor-fr

Query Parameters

limit  integer optional  

To limit of entities.

perPage  int optional  

Number of entities to return in a page.

page  int optional  

Page number to return, 1 by default

GET Book collection latest entries.

WITH PAGINATION

Get all Books ordered by date 'created_at'.

Route name: api.v1.books.latest

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books/latest?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books/latest"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/books/latest',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

    --header "Accept: application/json"

GET Count.

Get count of entities for a selected collection. Available for Book, Serie and Author.

Route name: api.v1.count

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/count?entities=author%2Cbook%2Cserie&languages=fr%2Cen" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/count"
);

const params = {
    "entities": "author,book,serie",
    "languages": "fr,en",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/count',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'entities'=> 'author,book,serie',
            'languages'=> 'fr,en',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

POST Send submission.

Route name: api.v1.submission.send

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/send/submission" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"ut\",
    \"email\": \"calista06@example.net\",
    \"honeypot\": true,
    \"message\": \"swgyfmvcrmtumu\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/send/submission"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "ut",
    "email": "calista06@example.net",
    "honeypot": true,
    "message": "swgyfmvcrmtumu"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/send/submission',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'name' => 'ut',
            'email' => 'calista06@example.net',
            'honeypot' => true,
            'message' => 'swgyfmvcrmtumu',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

content-type: application/json

    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/search"
);

};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

    "Content-Type": "application/json",

};

    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Request      

GET api/v1/series/{author_slug}/{serie_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author series' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to series' list and not authors' list, example: bordage-pierre

serie_slug  string  

slug of serie in meta.slug series' list, example: rohel-fr

GET Book collection of Serie.

Books list from one Serie, find by slug.

Route name: api.v1.series.show.books

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/series/books/delaney-joseph/lepouvanteur-fr?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/series/books/delaney-joseph/lepouvanteur-fr"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/v1/series/books/delaney-joseph/lepouvanteur-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
